***grootbrengen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grootbrengen.html>grootbrengen</a> (17847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>groot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">big, great, <a href = vnd.unilang:adult.html>adult</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brengen.html>brengen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grootbrengen.html>grootbrengen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To raise, bring up (a) young(<a href = vnd.unilang:ster.html>ster</a>)(s), from infancy to maturity</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To educate, rear, school, <a href = vnd.unilang:coach.html>coach</a> etc. offspring or other young <a href = vnd.unilang:charges.html>charges</a> on the path to <a href = vnd.unilang:adult.html>adult</a> life</li>
<li>the passive <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grootgebracht.html>grootgebracht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></b> means to grow up, mature (to majority)</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>groot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">great, big</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">city</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably calqued from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Großstadt</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grootstad.html>grootstad</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grootsteden.html>grootsteden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grootstad.html>grootstadje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A big/major city, up to a metropolis</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grot.html>grot</a> (3110)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">grotta</i> or indirectly <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">grotte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">crypta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κρυπτός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kruptós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:crypte.html>crypte</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krocht.html>krocht</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gruft</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***grotbewoner.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grotbewoner.html>grotbewoner</a> (117062)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grot.html>grot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewoner.html>bewoner</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">inhabitant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grotbewoner.html>grotbewoner</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grotbewoners.html>grotbewoners</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One (human or animal) who inhabits a cave; a troglodyte.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This largely lacks the primitive and prehistoric connotations of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:holbewoner.html>holbewoner</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">caveman, troglodyte</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
</body>

***grouchy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>grouchy</a> (42216)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>US 1895. From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grouch</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>. Originally US college student <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>grouchy</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">grouchier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">grouchiest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">originally college <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Irritable; easily upset; angry; tending to complain. <span class="defdate">[From 1895]</span>
<dl><dd><i>His boss <a href = vnd.unilang:gets.html>gets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>grouchy</a></b> when <a href = vnd.unilang:deadlines.html>deadlines</a> draw near.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1911</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jack_London" class="extiw" title="w:Jack London">London, <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>Jack</a></a>,  chapter III, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Abysmal_Brute/Chapter_III" class="extiw" title="s:The Abysmal Brute/Chapter III">The Abysmal <a href = vnd.unilang:brute.html>Brute</a></a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Not that young Pat <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a nasty temper, or <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>grouchy</a></b> as his father <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> feared.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1922</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sinclair_Lewis" class="extiw" title="w:Sinclair Lewis"><a href = vnd.unilang:lewis.html>Lewis</a>, Sinclair</a>,  chapter XXXI, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Babbitt/Chapter_31" class="extiw" title="s:Babbitt/Chapter 31">Babbitt</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> in to mumble that he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:sorry.html>sorry</a>, didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> mean to be <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>grouchy</a></b>," and to inquire as to her interest in movies.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1922</b>,  Fischer, <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> William,  “Author's Preface”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Abroad_with_Mark_Twain_and_Eugene_Field/Author%27s_Preface" class="extiw" title="s:Abroad with Mark Twain and Eugene Field/Author | s Preface">Abroad with Mark Twain and Eugene Field</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In Berlin I once <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> Susie Clemens—ill-fated, talented girl, who died so young—say to her father: "<b><a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>Grouchy</a></b> again! They <i>do</i> say that you can be funny when company <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> around—too bad that you don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> consider <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Fisher company."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cranky</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grumpy.html>grumpy</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">tetchy</span>; See also Thesaurus:irritable</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Old Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:guerra.html>guerra</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*werra</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*<a href = vnd.unilang:guerra.html>guerra</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*werra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">riot, disturbance, quarrel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*werrō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">confusion, disarray</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wers-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mix up, confuse, beat, thresh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">werra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">confusion, strife, quarrel</span><span title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">verwirren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to confuse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">werran</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to confuse, perplex</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">war</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">confusion, disarray</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:guerre.html>guerre</a> (75548)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:guerre.html>guerre</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">war</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:guerre.html>guerre</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">guere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">armed conflict between individuals or states, enmity, strife between individuals</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norman" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norman">Old Northern French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">werre</i>) from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*werra, *<a href = vnd.unilang:guerra.html>guerra</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*werra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">riot, disturbance, quarrel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*werrō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">confusion, disarray</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wers-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mix up, confuse, beat, thresh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">war</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">werra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">confusion, strife, quarrel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:ver.html>ver</a><i>wirren</i></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to confuse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">werran</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to confuse, perplex</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">war</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">confusion, disarray</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wyrsa, wiersa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">worse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren ***guilder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:guilder.html>guilder</a> (49406)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gulden.html>gulden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">golden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:guilder.html>guilder</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">guilders</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The former currency unit in the Netherlands, divided into 100 <a href = vnd.unilang:cents.html>cents</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1621</b>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:orders.html>Orders</a> and Articles Granted by the High and Mightie Lords the States General of the Vnited Provinces, Concerning the Erecting of a VVest Indian <a href = vnd.unilang:companie.html>Companie</a>: Together with the Priuiledges and Rights Giuen vnto the Same</cite>, [London |  s.n.], <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/84756820">84756820</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=SlvUAAAAMAAJamp;pg=PT19">clause 13</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">[N]one ſhall be choſen to be a Commiſſioner in the Court at <i>Amſterdam</i>, vnleſſe he put ſix thouſand <b>gilders</b> ſtocke of his owne in the ſaid <a href = vnd.unilang:companie.html>Companie</a>; [...]</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1743</b>,  [<a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lawson.html>Lawson</a>],  “The Manner in which <a href = vnd.unilang:strangers.html>Strangers</a> Live at the <i>Hague</i>”, in  <cite>A Description of Holland: Or, The Present State of the United Provinces.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Wherein is Contained, a Particular Account of The Hague, and All the Principal Cities and Towns of the Republick, with Their Buildings, Curiosities, amp;c. of the Manner and Customs of the Dutch; Their Constitution, Legislature, Sovereign Courts, Ministry, Revenue, Forces by Sea and Land, Navy, Admiralty, Bank, East-India Company, Navigation, Commerce, in Asia, Africa and America; and with Great-Britain, France, Spain, and the Other States of Europe. Their Universities, Arts, Sciences, Men of Letters, amp;c. To which are Added, Directions for Making the Tour of the Provinces.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite>, London |  Printed for J. and P. Knapton,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Crown in Ludgate-Street.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/1015399949">1015399949</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/descriptionofhol00londiala/page/208/mode/1up">page 208</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">On the <i>Spuy</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a good <i>Dutch</i> Inn, called the <i>Hoff <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:utrecht.html>Utrecht</a></i>. The Price <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>Gilder</b> a Day, or a <a href = vnd.unilang:shilling.html>Shilling</a> for the Dinner only.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>The former currency unit in Suriname, divided into 100 <a href = vnd.unilang:cents.html>cents</a>.</li>
<li>The current currency unit in the islands in the former Netherlands Antilles, divided into 100 <a href = vnd.unilang:cents.html>cents</a>.</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Obsolete spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gilder</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one who gilds</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1609</b> December (first performance)<b> | </b>,  Benjamin Jonson [<i>i.e.</i>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ben_Jonson" class="extiw" title="w:Ben Jonson"><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>Ben</a> Jonson</a>],  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Epic%C5%93ne,_or_The_Silent_Woman" class="extiw" title="w:Epicœne, or The Silent Woman">Epicoene, or The Silent Woman.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="A Comœdie. [...] you ſee <b>guilders</b> will not worke, but inclos'd. They muſt not diſcouer, how little ſerues, with the <a href = vnd.unilang:helpe.html>helpe</a> of art, to adorne a great <a href = vnd.unilang:dealen.html>deale</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***guile.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:guile.html>guile</a> (38239)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">gile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">gile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:guile.html>guile</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deception</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*wigila</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ruse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> Proto-Germanic with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wile</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:guile.html>guile</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">guiles</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Astuteness often marked by a certain sense of cunning or artful deception.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> April 24,  <a href = vnd.unilang:phil.html>Phil</a> Dawkes,  “Barcelona 2-2 Chelsea”, in  <cite>BBC Sport</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/sport/0/football/17817584">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a result that owed a lot to a <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:guile.html>guile</a></b> from Ramires but more to a display of <a href = vnd.unilang:guts.html>guts</a> from the Brazilian and his team-mates after <a href = vnd.unilang:terry.html>Terry</a>'s needless dismissal eight minutes before half-time for driving a knee into the back of Alexis Sanchez off the ball.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> November 11,  <a href = vnd.unilang:rory.html>Rory</a> Houston,  “Estonia 0-4 Republic of Ireland”, in  <cite>RTE Sport</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.rte.ie/sport/soccer/2011/1111/estonia_ireland_report.html">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Estonia <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> struggling to get to <a href = vnd.unilang:grips.html>grips</a> with the game while Ireland <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> showing a composure and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:guile.html>guile</a></b> that demonstrated their experience in <a href = vnd.unilang:play-off.html>play-off</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ties.html>ties</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Deceptiveness, deceit, fraud, duplicity, dishonesty.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. Newly Translated out of the Originall Tongues: amp; with the Former Translations Diligently Compared and Reuised, by His Maiesties Speciall Comandement. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gul.html>gul</a> (7075)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain. Probably cognate with West Frisian <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">gol</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of heart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Middle English <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:gulle.html>gulle</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">friendly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gulden.html>gulden</a> (15307)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">guldijn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">guldin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gulden.html>gulden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*guldīn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gulþīnaz</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goud.html>goud</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, replaced in modern Dutch with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gouden.html>gouden</a></i>.
